    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    model_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_accuracy FLOAT NOT NULL
);

    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,

    dataset_size INT NOT NULL,
    dataset_link VARCHAR(255)
);

    project_name VARCHAR(255),
    description TEXT,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE ai_users (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(255),
    email VARCHAR(255),
    role VARCHAR(50),
    registered_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE ai_models (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    model_name VARCHAR(255),
    description TEXT,
    algorithm VARCHAR(255),
    created_date DATE
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,

    description TEXT,
    size_mb INT,
    created_date DATE
);

    model_name VARCHAR(255),
    description TEXT,
    algorithm VARCHAR(255),
    created_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE ai_research_papers (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(255),
    author VARCHAR(255),
    abstract TEXT,
    publication_date DATE
);

    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE
);
